<Time>1545172651583< /Time>< rating>

< text>
I have found the personal assistance and knowledge given at Room to Grow to be Excellent! The recent advancements made horticulture are vast. To have an all in one place for supplies and solid advise by all involved, sets a standard not normally found in contemporary venues.
The other (and may I add, very important) aspect is price. Their prices surprisingly are very competitive with Amazon products and the other hydroponic store (located in Palmdale). Since their prices are very competitive, it gives the customer the advantage to immediately pick up your badly needed supplies in the event you can't wait (for online delivery).
I am a supporter of small business. Not for the sake of keeping this type of business alive, but because small business has the best knowledge and service needed for those who take their endeavors seriously.
I have sought advice many times from RTG. The results have been 100% correct. I have saved money by taking advantage of their years of experience.
I don't write reviews. However, coming from the retail side of customer service, I can appreciate excellent service. This review was very necessary.
Oh yeah, the owner even wrote a book on the subject of Indoor Growing. Buy a book, and get it autographed by the business owner. You can't do better than that!<//text>

< review>
First time renting a boat (electric 12 seater):

1. Called 1 week earlier to reserve (they answer from an office on docks so it rings for a bit before reaching someone)

2. An employee called 3 days prior to confirm reservations

3.showed up at the appointment time to sign some paperwork (takes less than 3 minutes).

4. Got on the boat and got a quick briefing and signed another document

5. Got pushed off the dock, enjoyed the experience, and was helped back to the dock.

No hassle, easy to do business with, and straightforward company @ a reasonable price.< /review>

<userid>112226550038608625491</userid><Name>Noah Bell</Name>< time>
1549672596920<//time>
<rating>5<//rating>< Review>
I had seen the fleet of Hopper boats for years around the Channel Islands Harbor and only just recently decided to check it out for myself. I was in for quite a surprise as were my guests. I brought 5 friends and the plan was to spend a couple hours during the holiday season to check out the decorated boats and houses in the area. Sarah (owner and operator) accommodated my group and from the get go everything was very professional in a relaxed atmosphere. The boat we rented was clean and surprisingly good condition considering some of the antics that I had seen other clients performing throughout the years. All care had been provided to ensure that we were well informed and comfortable in the operation and safety of "Current Affair". The time on the water went without a single adverse incident, and for me, was an awesome and convenient way for me to entertain my out of town friends on a budget ($65/hour plus well deserved tip was $30/person). Alcohol was allowed, another bonus, and the only drawback and reason we didn't use 3 hours is the total lack of public use docks and bathrooms in the harbor! Upon our return, Sarah was waiting for us in order to take any remaining guess work out of the equation- docking a boat is one of the most underrated ways to feel like a pro, and with Sarah's assistance, we were able to avoid the loud crunch I hear all the time during the summer, and instead were quickly tied to the cleats and helped out (a couple of us needed the help to be sure). All on all, an excellent experience that will have me coming back again! Cheers!<//Review>

I had an appointment to treat a recent gout flare. The entire visit lasted 2.5hrs which was relatively short for an urgent care visit. The registration process went smoothly and the front desk staff (Justin?) was very courteous. I am even more impressed with the medical staff (medical assistant and PA, thanks!) for their excellent bed manners and professionalism. The proposed treatment turned out to be very successful and the gout problem was solved within 48 hours. The only small shortcoming is that ActionCare does not support patient login accounts so I cannot conveniently retrieve my visit records online.</Text>

I had two visits to Action Urgent Care.
04/28/2021:
- Patient Intake/Receptionist: Elena DL is calm but warm, keeps you informed and makes you feel welcome. She was efficient and thoughtful, and remembered me right away at my next visit. Elena is wonderful as the first person you meet at Action Urgent Care!
- Dylan compassionate, professional, knowledgeable, and thorough. He listened to me patiently and thoroughly noted all of my conditions, which really helped put me at ease. He is absolutely in the exact right profession!
- Yasmin Kanlioglu was also incredibly professional, skilled, effective, but also caring and warm. I wish I could have hugged her!
At a time of incredible nerve pain and feeling vulnerable and overwhelmed, particularly as this was my very first visit to Action Urgent Care, I was so grateful to have encountered such exceptional and qualified care.

04/29/2021:
- I encountered Dylan again, and he once again took great care of me. I was not in as much pain as the night before and was able to get a good night's sleep for the first time in nearly two weeks, thanks to his and Yasmin's care. I could tell that Dylan really did genuinely feel relieved and happy to see that I had had some improvement in health.
- E. Engelhaupt-
She was incredibly thoughtful, fully aware of my recent background and concerns, and followed up on every pertinent detail to ensure my care continued. I felt comfortable and confident in her care.<//Text>

< review>
I found them via the mobile app Kyla, to get a COVID test.

First the mobile app.  The set up is simple enough for the situation, even though the insurance card verification fails the first time I tried for no apparent reasons.  the process of securing an appointment is both intuitive and frustrating - the automated part of going through the routine questions is very easy to follow, the problem arises when you have to interact with a human, first a provider to ascertain your eligibility, then a nurse to actual schedule the appointment.  you tend to have to wait several minutes for either of them to show up, and it's hard to pay attention to the phone all that time, if you miss the human response by a few minutes, you'll have to restart the process again.  Also, even though the app says 9am-8pm, they seem to stop responding at around 7pm instead.  the combination of having to wait for minutes for human response, and having to restart if you don't respond right away, makes the experience frustrating.

Now the positives - I was able to secure an appointment within 24 hours both times I tried, the test site I use is drive through, staff is friendly and professional, the process is quick and painless, and the best part, the results came back the same day at 11pm, both times.  thumbs up.</review>

I went here for a medical condition because my primary physician's office is closed during weekends and I don't want to go to the ER since my situation is not that serious based on my self evaluation. Its structure (which may look small) is at the parking lot near the mall, shops and apartments. Upon entering, you'll find  a well lit wide receiving area with plenty of seats lined up for waiting patients. They will first gather your medical history, measure your weight, height and take your blood pressure. The in-house physician will diagnose your symptoms, electronically prescribe medication directly to your preferred pharmacy and send you off with a firm assurance that you'll be feeling better. <rate>5</rate>< text>
The food is excellent and the owners are very hospitable. Its not a formal dining place, service would between a deli / restuarant setting. The host will check on the guests frequently but works in the kitchen. However, they are very friendly and welcoming.
Weekdays lunch buffet is good. Limited choice of meat, rice and vegetables dishes, but, quality and taste is good. You can also order from their regular menu. Once you eat here, you will return again and again.
The grocery store is right beside it where you get fresh meat and Afghani bread (the long flat bread). Both the grocery store and restaurant is owned by the same establishment.</text>

<text>Site For Sore Eyes is absolutely Outstanding!  Yes, they have really cool styles (I found at least 6 pair I Loved - which doesn't ever happen) and every name brand that would make a eyeglass aficionado feel like they won the lottery. But it is the exemplary staff that has won my loyalty - for life. The moment I walked in, Grace's open smile along  with her graciousness immediately made me feel at ease. You see, I wasn't there for eye glasses this time. I had accidentally stepped on my favorite, and yes, chichi expensive sunglasses - and for me, it felt dire; with light colored eyes, I literally cannot see in the sun thus spend $$$$ on good sunglasses. <rating>4<//rating>< review>
Well you have to start off by realizing this is Ridgecrest! It's on us-395 somewhere between nowhere and somewhere. But it is a long way to any other dog parks so it is nice to have this break if you're heading up 395. The park is well fenced there are a lot of big shade trees the only real concern I would warn you about is that it doesn't appear in Ridgecrest that you were required to pick up your dog's poop if it's anywhere near a fence. So the perimeter of the park is lined with biological landmines. But it has grass, and it is in the middle of nowhere. So this part is definitely a 4 or a little above star<//review>

The only bummer is that their flights are pre-set and you cannot make substitutions.  Even so, the flights that they do offer are fairly well put together.  Would definitely return when back in San Francisco.</text>

<user>109620987767531213231< /user>< username>
Jing Yu</username>
<Date>1486098708170<//Date>< Rating>
5<//Rating>
<Review>The Crafty fox is a tidy, cozy and lovely pub owned by a few friendly Irish guys.  This used to be my favorite neighborhood bar back when I lived in the Mission - unfortunately it's a bit of a distance for me now, but I still stop be for old times sake.

The beer selection is one of the BEST in the city. There are around 34+ beers on tap with a focus on the local craft beer scene - special emphasis on Almanac and Fieldwork. Crafty also has flights according to taste, but I would defer to getting a pint of the knowledgable bartenders recommendations as the flights seem a little over priced.

Craft ambiance is clean, whimsical (a little old world) with a long copper bar top, wooden interior and naked Edison lightbump fixtures. I love the casual, low-key vibe, that can make any patron feel comfortable - especially after a couple of their beers. Pedro, the head chef, used to buy fresh flowers from the farmers market every week - which were a beautiful, bright addition to the bar.

The food is SF pricing but solid all around. You can spend a pretty penny on food if you try to do a full dinner. I always default to the kennebec fries (because few snacks go better with a beer than fries) which are reasonably priced at $6 for their size but I typically chose to eat elsewhere for my entree. Food options in the mission are abundant.</Review>< pics>
None< /pics>
